de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints comes from moisture that has expanded to every part of the body, and when pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and remedies of medicines do not cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: make the cut on the outside of the joint, and the cauterization should be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is necessary that you prick the face with a sharp object, then perform the cauterization on the entire cauterization as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	If the pain comes to the joints and other parts of the body, and this happens many times, then cauterize each joint III or IV of each part on all olive cauterization; and if you have skill for more, but do not hold your hand too long as much as it hurts.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	If the pain descends to the joints and back, apply the cauterization we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	When the pain is in the hands, if it continues for a while, I make points on both lines of the frost; and if there is no more pain, I make points at each joint and at the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes from the wrists or shoulders, I cauterize each part, and give the patient medicine and government to the midwife.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make the midwife give medicine and purge the poison, she will be healthy in the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes with groans, and the blood drops down in streams, and it is new, if it comes to your notice that when you cure it, it will not leave the other side; and that it uses things that lighten the belly, if it descends from its belly; then make it lie on its back between your hands, and command it to lick its own tail as much as it can, and draw it towards your two hands, and sign with a circle around the bone of the other shoulder, and in all signs that it resembles a half circle around the other side; then wash the cauterization with the form of the cauterization:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and has a taste.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the dirt from your leg; and the surgeon will touch his hand to ensure they do not return; and work well on the thighs with the patient, and put the cauterization sign on all your hand, and hold it straight and as far as you can reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again until you touch the bone; and be careful that the dirt does not seep out when you make the cauterization, that you do not burn it; and so that the patient does not die or suffer from other wounds.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone with the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterization of children be done subtly according to the size of the bone, and large people as large; after three days, care for the child's head with a burn so that the pain is eased; after treating other wounds as long as they are healthy, and gently touch his back for as long as the wound is well-sored; and it is necessary that his nails be kept long, so that the excrement does not come out when he goes to sleep in rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, he will find a well-made girdle around him, and after forty more days; then he should rest, so that he can work quickly and avoid excessive drunkenness and vileness, and excessive braiding; and when he makes this teaching, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not increase, if the cauterization is done according to its quantity, and according to the third angle of this form; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the ancients has said that it should be cauterized at three angles according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But the first sign of the bone is the fracture and draw a line for the length of the rupture, and another for the width, and hold the patient's hand tightly at all points of the cauterization claw.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	However, the first cauterizations are more gentle and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of pain in no member.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any member, whether from cold or wounding, and this pain lasts long, and the cure with medicine is not enough, then it must be cauterized at the cauterization called "points", and the cauterization according to the length of the member, its width, its strength, its virtue, its location of torsions and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first burn is not deadly, it's well; if the name is different, continue with another burn on that part, because it is customary that one must die at the member that it is directed to, but if the patient is alive, then you should make the burns as many as necessary for the patient to be healthy.
de meselerie	of malediction
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The curses are never helped by burning once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the burning, when the disease is at its beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not delay or tire, and you doubt that corruption will corrupt all the patient, then I make the burns on the head: I cut off the head, and the other towards the front at the end of the cheeks; and they touch the corners, and the heel to the hips; and I let your hand as much as the burn goes to the bone, and as much as the pus comes out so that the vapors of the large humors can come out; and you cauterize on the mouth according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	When the burning is everywhere scarce; and it manifestly appears, if you cauterize the wound with these cauteries that we have mentioned or chief, and the cauterization in one place, and the cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and on the spine of the back, and on the crupper and the other parts, and the shoulders, and the wrists, and the tendons of the fingers, and all the joints of the hands and feet, and the fissures of the hands; and you wear bandages that are placed behind the burns, which are not burned, so that you do not burn them; and never once has a cauterization been made on the bone of the elbow, and the other on the stomach bone, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When more you burn, the more help you give, and profit from it; and advise the patient that the patient does not feel pain in the burn if it is as healthy as it should be, because the heart is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the burn be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the head with flour several times with honey and other remedies as long as it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any part and is cured with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the burn is made on the member according to its size and thickness; and let the burn be entered into the side of the ear; then the care of ointments as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	1. And no time is made when cauterized on the hand, arm, and back, at the end of the nerve that is silent to the member, and if it is not enflamed; and none enters if it is not known of the members and the issues of the moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	2. Of scars
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	3. When the disease called "scars" is awakened, and the art of medicine does not help, then cauterize with a cautery once or twice, according to the amount of the vesicle, as long as the blister is ointed and has its color; then use flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and scabs of colon and almond, of each part; and mix all together, and wrap it with a cloth, and apply to the body as much as it is needed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore first appears, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done at the cauterization point that seems to be a circle, then turn it completely around the entire sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the wise ones say that cauterization is done in the environment of the sore; and it seems to me that this is not the best, because I fear that it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have always wanted this to happen once; and the most appropriate thing is that it is cauterized around, at the cauterization point called "circle", if as we have said, cauterization is done.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the inflammation that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	If any have a disease called "adubelati", and it lags in measuring either due to excessive discharge or because the patient's condition becomes too weak (that is, too many) and there is little blood, or for other reasons, you see it lagging in measuring: therefore, the cauterization is performed by inserting small cauterizing pins as they are pricked; afterwards, they are left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will lag in measuring.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it lagging in measuring, if the cauterization is hot and this form is not suitable,
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization is perceived by the ear, and it is such that the patient feels pain in a certain way that the course of the sweat is agile.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, if it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cauterization by fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a mangy of the limb, because it eats the limbs as much as it does the dry sticks.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauterization by fire, then sharpen the cauterization claws according to what is needed in the leg where the disease is; after cauterizing all parts as much as possible, there will be nothing left of it, that everything that is corrupted is not osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil as much as the burned eschar is large, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the care of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If you see after three days that healthy burns do not appear, it is good; and if not, continue the cauterization on the parts that are still corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	This remedy has never been cured by medical treatment in the place of fire cauterization; but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said the cure of the medicine ague in the division: take what you have skill in.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the pores that come as pimples
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that the pimples are caused by inflammation, which is called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that darkens the skin.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is known as fire cauterization, and hot iron cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is when you heat the iron and press it onto the skin, like a pin of fire, and it is made of red-hot iron according to the size that can burn through all parts, and has fine margins; after that, you put everything on the nail, and turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the point of the nail; and it leaves three days before it starts to secrete sweat; then you make a poultice of well-cooked mugwort with milk, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nails will become unrooted from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the wound with ointment as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	If the wound becomes infected many times in the hands and fingers, then and only then is it necessary to perform a cauterization with hot iron; and it should be done in this way: take a piece of iron or steel, or a thorn, and fasten it to the nail and the althelul, which is to cover warts; then place the iron so that it burns everything around, then put a little hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn until the edge of the iron touches the root of the nail, and find the hot water way perfectly at the root; then suffer the pain of the hot iron for a little while, then let it fall, and it will all fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I will create another step, as long as you are able to handle all of these, then cure the wounds that have been inflicted with fire.
li cure dou trembler	I will cure you so you do not tremble.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If you tremble from cold, or fever, or other causes, it is necessary that you have four cauteries or four spikes, one between each spike; and one spike at the top of the stomach, and the others in the olive oil; if this helps to stop the trembling, and cure the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pimples that have been inflicted with fire.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	For no time do blisters or pustules appear on the body, which come from large corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to cauterize as soon as they appear, use a subtle cautery made of martial pitch, or the point can be held in the fire, or the cautery of Aristotle's root, or the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And never have the cauteries been made at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and they do not grow new wounds in front, but are destroyed by the superfluity that comes, and they are cured; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the arrow is seized
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times, great dislocations of blood from the arrow that is seized at the wound which comes to the pardefuers, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the member, and such things; and it is a great grief to open.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And when there is none, if you have to put your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it tight until it is calmed by your thumb, and does not cause pain; then heat the olive-oil cauteries more or less according to the size of the wound, and I will do it myself or according to the size of the wound and the lesion on the limb and the arrow that is routed, and place the cautery on the vein where you hold your thumb, and hold the cautery as long as it is not re-injured.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If it is hot when you tighten the vein with your child's head, and the cautery ends, then quickly take another cautery that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue doing this one after the other until the nerve is not inflamed, and no other harm comes to the patient; and be cautious that when without cutting the artery, you can hardly endure the pain immediately when the artery is large, if it is not by one of the four methods we have mentioned: by cauterization or extraction when it is properly treated, or by gentle twisting, or by medicines placed on it that may cause inflammation; and let it be tied and extracted.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will carefully manage the remaining of the thread, or to put things burning on, or other similar things, should not profit from it if not.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is none, and no good or bad medicine is present, then he should put his index on the wound of the vein as we have said, and firmly press until it is sore from the wound and the vein; and he should not move, but rather let it be cold often that it is not frozen and swollen and sore; and make inquiries about those who are skilled in cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	For the first chapter of medicine, we have told you about all diseases that require cauterization with fire or burning, and their causes, effects, and forms of cauterization; and I will go to this chapter as my own way because it is lighter to handle than the other.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	However, before I begin this, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauterizations, and for this reason greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	I warn you not to attempt foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If they come from those who are so attached to their disease that they die easily by the severity of their disease and its greatness; and from these we should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And there are those who understand you and say, "Wait, I am coming"; and the disease is unscrupulous.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It only requires that you allow those who come to you to have this manner, but put more respect in your honor than in your covetousness, and do not give in too easily but wisely of what you are certain, and what you can take; and use prophecy and indication in the cures of your diseases for the health of the patient; and this will help to your good reputation, glory, and memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very fine thread, our Lords give you understanding and straightness, and if you wish to hope for the holy inspiration of her hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have commanded this chapter in stating that it is a cauterization, according to the cauterizations, which I have commanded for the chief joints, because you will find it more lightly than other things.
dou chief plein d’aigue	dough, chief full of acid
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Scars that this disease comes from the children many times in the mother, and when it is pulled too hard on the child's head; and never has it come from a cured cause that it is not.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease occur in adults, and in all the cases I have seen, death followed; and for this reason I think it is worthwhile to briefly mention some treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I have seen children of this age, and the head grew larger each day until it could no longer support itself; and it was thought that it was due to moisture, and this moisture is assembled between the skull and the sinus, from the ear to the skull; and the dislocations are such that when the skull is moved, the most painful spots are found between the ear and the skull, and the abscesses are small, so that you can cut out the child's head with a wide incision; and so long as the moisture increases, this form of the disease will be present.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more intense, and the abscess is larger, if I make these cuts in the manner of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is deep into the bone, and you see the commissures of each part of the chest tightened, and the water gushes out when you press on it with your hand, and this has not been done before: then it may be that you cut through the chest III times according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.

After removing the dressings and powders, and applying wine and oil, and letting it remain for five days; then remove it, and cure the wound with bandages and poultices, and make the chest even, and then grease the dry meat with as little moisture as possible until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is to look at or open the large opening of the abscess, and the assembled angle; for it is never in front; never behind; never to the right; and never to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Measure the size of the abscess opening and the angle of the wedge, and they are made according to what you have; and do not block the artery; and come out with blood, if the patient dies from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	from remedy

de emigrainne	The first line of the text is "de emigrain
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the head aches and is hot, and there are gouts of blood and tears in the temples, and the pain becomes severe, and it is treated with medicines and all sorts of remedies, but they do not help, then we cut the arteries of the temples and cauterize, as we have experienced.

puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés. des larmes	of tears.

dou reume des eulz	This translates to: "He pulls out the hairs.
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees; et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue; adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	This translates to: "If no bloodletting is practiced regularly, and you see the hairs growing long and thin, and the eyes wandering, and the papers burned; and the hair falls out, and there is great pain in the head, and the patient is weak; therefore, one should be cautious of these accidents, as these materials and this bloodletting only serve to weaken the body, and the cure that follows is this.

de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the ear drum
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses: ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer; ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois; ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	All that is in the ears is one of the four things: grains, stones, mines, or similar things; or seeds, like beans, peas, and chickpeas; or things that flow, like acorns and almonds, and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When he pierces the ear drum or any other part of the ear that does not fit well, or grows in the ear, he should put the ear to the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction; et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine; et estent l’oreille au desus.	If you see the wound, and there is no drop of violet oil or linseed oil, then extract it; I make the wound clean, and the patient sneezes as they extract, and put a piece of cloth or thread into the ear; and the ear becomes plugged.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure; et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	This treatment is often successful; and if it does not work, then the patient must undergo extraction with forceps, and the form is as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin; se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure; et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne; puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit; et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor; puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	If it jumps with the forceps, it is wrong; and if not, then undergo extraction with a small double forceps; and if it does not jump with this, then make a loop of thread and pull the end of the tail or ear hole, and plug it with wax so that it cannot enter with the loop; then the treatment is formed, as we have said, since it often comes out in this way; and if it does not come out in this way, then take some glue on your fingers and put any instrument that can be used to do this without causing pain, and put a piece of cotton inside; then press the glue on the wound or whatever it is, and treat.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme; et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant; et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche; et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If she does not flee from all these things that we have said, and if you continue to force the ear even though it is swollen and spasmodic, and the manner of forcing it is that you first make the patient of the head more comfortable with the salve, according to the measure of its virtue, then hold the patient's head between your hands and turn the ear away from the wind, and make a small prick at the root of the ear in the grease or where it depends; and let the prick be as a moon, as you go towards the point, then the bone will according to your strength, and the salve will hasten to your mouth; and the cure so long as it is healthy.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction; et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	If it is a grain that is in and it swells, then apply an extraction; if it cannot be excreted, then apply the spumous substance according to this form.
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and apply an incision to that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces; puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	But do not cut it if you think the grain is moist from the earwax, as long as you have done many pieces; then extract it with soft pincers and honey, as we have said, if the extractions are soothing.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the ear, therefore, if the grain is in the ear, then the surgeon should use the first condyles for exsternum, and ample the ear with soft cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let there be scarring on the same ear or the eye.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps for this, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu; et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille; et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer; et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars; puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	And if it does not jump, then take many piercings according to the length of your nail, and sharpen them a little at the fire; and put the forceps on one side of the ear, and pull out through the other part, and make one more hole on the hole that is in the ear; and continue making holes one after another until the eye is all out, and then it will all be out; and if you see, if it jumps, and take one of the ears, and the other one hold on fire as long as the lesser jump is hotter; then make another part of other jumps as long as the eye is all out, according to what we have said in the hole.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division; mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures; et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	In the extraction of the tooth, if it is small in size, similar to a pea and resembles something else, it can be treated as we have described in the division; but if it is large in size, it can be felt, and it is the lighter thing to handle compared to the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil: s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	In the extraction of the ears' jewelry, if you treat it as we have described in the division and use distillations, but the treatment does not work, if you look at the ear to the sun: if there are no openings, if you gently pull out the pliers, and if there are, if you take the rope from here, it is the form.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be tight and wide.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine; fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	And bite the more subtle part of the ear according to the amount of suffering the patient endures, then all together will form a cain; do this often as much as you can.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere; et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations; et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if they do not listen to it, then let them be placed in the corner of the cloth as I have said in the incision; and if they do not soil it as we have said, then administer distillations that the ancients have used in the decision of the verse, and you will find or mix your oils and medicines in the ear at this instrument; and if you distill your oils and medicines in the ear according to what you see:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller; et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton; puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille; puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille; et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille; et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	1. And let silver or gold be boiled in the wounds as many times as possible to draw out the poison; and use a proper distillation instrument made of silver, and if you see the rasor and envelop it at the end of the cotton; then let your oil or juice gush out, and whatever you see of your medicines in the cainne, and the cainne is in the ear; then dip the rasor into all the cotton, and press your hand firmly until the oil is distilled or comes from the ear; and it will feel cold to the patient, and so is the distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille; and keep it not too cold, for the medicine will not be effective if it is too cold.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the ear's chill
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles; et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir; et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	No child is born without having a cold in the ears; and this very same thing happens due to ear pain or a cut in the ear, and there is no sign of cold in the ear at all times, unless one can see; and never has there been a pus in the ear that was not visible.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil; et regarde dedens: se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	If that which comes forward is not visible, it is a sign of recovery in many cases, and then you must put the ear with the cold in the sun; and look: if you see the ophthalmia apparent, then this is the form of the spume:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille; se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	And let it be and stretch it all over and under until it does not cause pain; if the inflammation is on the ear or the ear's side, if you have gentle forceps and a light cope, as long as the forceps are entirely covered.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the inflammation is on the edge of the ear, if you have a gentle rasp and a light cope, then you heat it slightly and place it on the ear's side.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille; puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	If you feel the inflammation that the patient feels in his ear, gently rasp, and do not burn the ear's nerves; then put a tent according to the large puncture, and apply Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet; et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. Do not cause any pain as much as the wound is sore, or take a tent and moisten it with hot rose water, and sprinkle some powdered vitrol; and if you see the ear covering, then roll up the tent and move another soft tent made of olive oil and wax, as long as the ear is sore. Then the doctor when he is healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	2. And if the blood comes out, then dip a sponge and wet it with cold water, and put it on the ear, and use other treatments that stop the flow of blood which are treated with distillations.
de la char des papieres	The first sentence to translate is "Or cautere de feu comande
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines; puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues; et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines; et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	When the cautery is not done, if the cauterization of the subtle curved cauterizing iron is made, and the cauterizer after the incision does not cause any harm; and they are often repaired, with nothing to deter them from their roots; and when those roots are burned by fire, they are dead and do not return.
de la gresle	of the grit
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz; li ovraiges est telz: pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir; fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Many times, papers come from the hairs things that seem gritty in their form and hardness, and for this it is called "snow" or "grandine", and it is an assembly of large moisture in the paper on both sides; the treatment is as follows: first, if the snow is silent on one side and the other, it is a light thing to know; then make it wide, then scrape off each part lightly, then take tweezers, and close.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide; et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee; et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	1. If you do not perceive a piece of paper with your hand, it does not matter if it hurts; and if the wound is large, if it assembles into a stitch, and the cure as long as it is healthy; and if it is small, if it does not make any force, because the restoration of the other parts is enough.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre; et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien; et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	2. If the snow is descending towards the earhole of the ear, if reversed, and the snow is held with forceps, and it presses from both sides; and if the paper is moved away by incision, it does not hurt; and when the snow is pressed, if the salty oil is leaked, and the wound is cured as much as the patient is healthy.
de la graisse des eulz	Of the fat of the hairs
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz; et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	Exinach is a grease that is obtained by tearing paper into thin strips, and this is done more often as children grow older, and it causes pain to their hair, and they come to the catharre in the mornings, and cannot look at the light of the sun because their tears are on their hair; and because they sleep with their faces down, and they sleep on their pillows that are damp from the moisture that the oil spreads over them.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press your hand on your head and feel the exinach inside.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain; et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li; et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle; puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne; et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach; et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	1. And the manner of the cautery is that the patient places his head in your hand; then take a cloth from linen, and make a tent according to the quantity contained in each part, then place it on top; and press with your two hands on both sides, so that the cautery is assembled in the circle; then make a mucous environment of the moisture at the anus, trenchant a large fissure, not larger than the wound you make at the gash of the vein; and make the skin thick enough that you can see the cautery; and in other positions, the cautery comes out of the fissure, according to the shape of a piece of greasy white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars; et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	1. Remove the thorn from all pieces of sheet hanging between your two cheeks, and turn your hand to the right and left as much as it is possible; and make sure you do not push in the furrow, that you do not go to all the stomach, that you do not squeeze.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere; puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	2. If the thorn does not open at the beginning of the furrow, then lightly open it as much as it appears; then remove it as we have said, and wet the sheet in the water and in the oil, and put it on the cheek, and press gently.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	3. And if such men who have hairy scalps put on oil to corrupt the moisture that is dried.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the cure, as long as he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the patient comes to the aid of an abscess, if the doctor uses cleansing ointments as long as he is healthy.
des poilz des papieres	of the papers' hairs
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz; et est li cure selonc IIII manieres: ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	When papers grow hairs other than their nature, and are awakened, if they harm the eyes, and bring about diseases such as tears and mollifications of the paper and albugine, as long as it is caused by the destruction of the hairs; and the cure is done in four ways: either by burning together with fire, or by medicine according to what is before or in the chapter of cauterization, and is made by cutting and stitching or by needles, according to what I will say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre; s’elle est convertie, c’est boin; se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus; et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur; puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit; puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	It is necessary that you place the head of the patient's shoulder in your hand, then turn the paper of the oil to your left hand; if it is converted, it is well; if not, then insert an awl into all the threads of the filament; and let the margin of the paper or the hair that grows from these hairs be on the left side of the paper, and turn the filament to the right at the paper; then cut off the part of the paper, the hairs adjusted, throughout the entire circumference, from the largest to the smallest; then pull out the filament, and put a small tent of cloth and drapery on the paper, then sew a figure on the paper according to the quantity that you see rising the paper that is marked with dots; and it will be necessary that the figure is according to the amount that you see rising the paper that is marked with dots.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie; puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit; et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute; puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce; et si a une autre maniere: et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	If a part of the body that is skilled at handling paper does not bear much weight, then cut out all the lines you have written, and start with large, firm scars just a little bit; and one of the furnaces near the natural hair growth in length, then burn the root at one of the two angles, then scrape it off completely; then assemble the two lips together with a sewing needle at every thread of fine wool, and draw out the sand, and make the superfluity of threads from the two corners of anything glutinous, if you see this done; and if not, then leave the stitching and the threads just until three or four; then cure the wound with the stitching of things that are dried and constricted, because the paper relaxes under the pain of the wound and its assembly, but the stitching is rotten (as they say the ancients), and it is overwhelmed with fear; and if another way: and if you see the paper of a figure that is as such as the fur of a mouse, according to the form that is here: then cut out all the lines you have written, and start with large, firm scars just a little bit; and one of the furnaces near the natural hair growth in length, then burn the root at one of the two angles, then scrape it off completely; then assemble the two lips together with a sewing needle at every thread of fine wool, and draw out the sand, and make the superfluity of threads from the two corners of anything glutinous, if you see this done; and if not, then leave the stitching and the threads just until three or four; then cure the wound with the stitching of things that are dried and constricted, because the paper relaxes under the pain of the wound and its assembly, but the stitching is rotten (as they say the ancients), and it is overwhelmed with fear.
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then comes the one who surpasses with equal strength according to the form that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure; et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment; puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans; et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit: si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision; mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	And if you cannot hold the nails, and the thing is not equal, then take a needle or a thread, and draw it out; and take another thread of about the same length as the large one, and the small one, and assemble the threads evenly between your two hands; then gently press with your hand, and gently stitch all the leather where you have sewn, as we have experienced, then assemble the lips of the wound by stitching, and treat it until it is healthy; and when the suture comes to your incision, if the pain and swelling are alleviated; and never has there been that the hair of the paper has turned: if you use what we have said about the incision; but the stitching on both sides is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme: et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est; et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz; puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment; et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui. dou derrompement de toile uvee	A sudden pulling or tearing of the eyeball
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir; adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier; et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition; puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef; et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee; et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	When a sudden disruption occurs in the eyeball, it opens and reveals paper like strands, as fine as resin grains; therefore, close your eyes and take hold of the eye socket, making a cut at the root of the part that is most affected by the injury, then make another cut where there is a double filament; and perceive, leave the first cut according to its position; then cut the double filament and take out a part of the eyeball, press it well, then remove the needle and put some ointment on the wound in abundance; and leave it until the threads are no longer attached to the eyeball, and cure the wound with comforting things as long as the wound is healed; and never leave a wound unattended by the eyeball, as long as it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost; puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the hairs grow long and even, if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the oil's gum
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue; et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz; puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit; et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	This disease called "alcunnati" is not other than a gum that is assembled in the oil, appearing as a wet descent, and it is not wet; and the manner of appearance of the wound if you make the patient sit upright and straight, then take the chief between your hands of II parts, and pull it as you see the gum coming to the eye of your hairs; then it is like a fish, and does not descend and does not become disentangled, and you see the malaides things as they were; and if it does not descend, say that it is wet, and if the descent of the gum is not apparent as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse; et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you place the patient's arm in your hands, then take a soft spatula and make a cut along the corneal edge as far as the continuation of the conjunctive with the cornea and the corneal ring, until the bow is out; and when it is out, let it drip into the cold, warm water mixed with honey, or cold and fenugreek is boiled and honey, then it should be cured by other means as long as it is healthy.
des aigues de l’oil	of the oils of the oil
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier; si en oevre selonc la santeit.	We have seen the appearances of the oils in the division, and when it is necessary to perceive; if according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort; puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres; puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre; puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide; et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour; et c’est li corone de l’oil; si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	1. It is necessary that you hold the patient's hand in front of your face, with the light of the sun, and the smooth and tight oil; then place the paper of the oil on your left hand, so that the hairs are on the right side, or on your right hand, the hairs are on the left side; then take in your right hand, with the hairs on the right side, the instrument called "almagda"; then place the tip of the instrument's point at the coronet through the largest part of the oil in the bladder of the oil in the smallest part; then push the instrument called "almagda" firmly, and twist your hand until it pierces the bladder of the oil, and feel that almagda viegne to the empty thing; and it is necessary that the measure of the almagda hole is at the end of the measure of the espaice which is on the prunele at the end of the nose; and this is the coronet of the oil; if you see the bone in that paper for the clarity of the cornered skin, and then place the instrument where it is, then press it with force through one hole after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the patient feels dizzy now, if they see the surgeon before them and the instrument in their hand.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc; et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	After resting for a little while, and if the patient feels dizzy again, open the second vein, take the forceps with the instrument, and when it is firmly held and does not move, gently twist your hand around the handle several times; then remove a piece of wool from the end of the candle, and pour the oil into it.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then pour the oil into the wounds or soft tissue, and mix it with healthy oil and a little urine, and apply it with the healthy oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those who are of our kin, put on shoes with many buttons.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the oil cannot enter through the hair because it is too hard, because there are too many men with very hard hair, then you must use the instrument called "alberit," which is shaped like this:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit; et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous; et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor; puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor; et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And pierce only the conjunctive, and do not pull too hard, but make a small incision, then bore further, as we have said; and at the completion of the work, the patient should lie down on his back in the dark room; and he should be given light foods, and not move his head to the right or left, and keep it according to its natural position; then he should lie down in this house, look at things, and make sure nothing is seen, and then put the bandage on after the ninth day; but it is necessary that you do this during the cure or after the incision now, but it is necessary that you put the bandage on, because the eye swells rapidly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme; et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	When the patient feels pain, move the oil in front of the seventh day, and address the one who calms the pain; and when it is pacified, remove the eye and put it in your face to cover any joint, and remain in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas; et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	Then, leave the house little by little, and become one's own disciple; and be aware that no students should intermingle in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens; et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	Then some came to us who were from the Yrach, who told us that in some ways it was a maggot perception, but we have never seen one on our land, nor have we ever heard of it in old books; and by chance, this is a new thing.
